Typeface 
 The Monotype Corporation plc. Data 
 The Monotype Corporation plc / Type Solutions Inc. 1990-91 All Rights ReservedCentury GothicRegularCentury Gothic Regular : 1991Century GothicVersion 2.30CenturyGothicCentury Gothic is a trademark of The Monotype Corporation plc.Monotype Typography, Inc.Monotype Type Drawing OfficeA design based on Monotype 20th Century, which was drawn by Sol Hess between 1936 and 1947. Century Gothic maintains the basic design of 20th Century but has an enlarged 'x' height and has been modified to ensure satisfactory output from modern digital systems. The design is influenced by the geometric style sans serif faces which were popular during the 1920's and 30's. Useful for headlines and general display work and for small quantities of text, particularly in advertising.http://www.monotype.com/html/mtname/ms_welcome.htmlhttp://www.monotype.com/html/designer/des_index.htmlNOTIFICATION OF LICENSE AGREEMENT

 The Monotype Corporation plc. Data 
 The Monotype Corporation plc / Type Solutions Inc. 1990-91 All Rights ReservedCentury GothicRegularCentury Gothic Regular : 1991Century GothicVersion 2.30CenturyGothicCentury Gothic is a trademark of The Monotype Corporation plc.Monotype Typography, Inc.Monotype Type Drawing OfficeA design based on Monotype 20th Century, which was drawn by Sol Hess between 1936 and 1947. Century Gothic maintains the basic design of 20th Century but has an enlarged 'x' height and has been modified to ensure satisfactory output from modern digital systems. The design is influenced by the geometric style sans serif faces which were popular during the 1920's and 30's. Useful for headlines and general display work and for small quantities of text, particularly in advertising.http://www.monotype.com/html/mtname/ms_welcome.htmlhttp://www.monotype.com/html/designer/des_index.htmlNOTIFICATION OF LICENSE AGREEMENT
